***brant.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:brant.html>brant</a> (65757)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:brand.html>brand</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*brandaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:brant.html>brant</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>fire</li>
<li>burning piece of wood</li>
<li>firewood, fuel</li>
<li>burn (mark on the skin or something else)</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = <i class="Zyyy mention" lang="und">*brahsmō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*brahsmǭ</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*brahsinō</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*brahsmaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bream</span><span class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*brehwanaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:shining.html>shining</a>, glittery, sparkly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European ***bree.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bree.html>bree</a> (14856)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">brewe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">bre</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">bregh</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">brēġ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">eyelid</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Anglian dialect</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>. Compare West Saxon <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">brǣw</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">brēaw</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">brēaġ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">eyelid</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*brēwō</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">(<a href = vnd.unilang:wenk.html>wenk</a>)brauw</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Braue</i>. Compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">brae</i> from the same source. Apparently related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">brow</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bree.html>bree</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">brees</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete or dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The eyelid.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete or dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The eyebrow.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The brow; forehead.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">bre</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:breien.html>breie</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">broth; gravy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, apparently from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">brīw</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">brīġ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pottage; porridge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*brīwaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">porridge; mash</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:brei.html>Brei</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brij.html>brij</a></i>. Alternatively, the word could be a cognate of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Brühe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">broth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">brüeje</i>, from the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">brüejen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to scald, boil</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*brōaną</i>, whence modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">brühen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:broeien.html>broeien</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">brȫjen</i>. This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> less likely, however, since the verb <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not attested in English nor in <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span>. Both paths eventually lead to the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> root <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰrewh₁-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to boil, toss, cook, brew</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">broth</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">brew</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bree.html>bree</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">brees</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete outside <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Broth.</li></ol>

***breedsprakig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:breedsprakig.html>breedsprakig</a> (94885)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">breedspraak</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:breedsprakig.html>breedsprakig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:breedsprakig.html>breedsprakiger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">breedsprakigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sometimes derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> elaborate and extensive in language, verbose</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:breken.html>breken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to break</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijzer.html>ijzer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">iron</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***breien.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:breien.html>breien</a> (15082)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:breiden.html>breiden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bregdan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bregdaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:breien.html>breien</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to knit</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***brein.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:brein.html>brein</a> (3238)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:brein.html>brein</a></i>, next to the more common <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bragen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bregen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bragan</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bregin</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bragną</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:brein.html>brein</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Bregen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Brägen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">brain</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***breinaald.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:breinaald.html>breinaald</a> (84554)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:breien.html>breien</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to knit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naald.html>naald</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">needle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:breinaald.html>breinaald</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:breinaalden.html>breinaalden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:breinaald.html>breinaaldje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">knitting needle</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***breken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:breken.html>breken</a> (1522)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">brēken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*brecan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*brekan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*brekaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰreg-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:breken.html>breken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ergative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to break</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:breuk.html>breuk</a></span></li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:brengen.html>brengen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">bringan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bringaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰrenk-</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:broke.html>broke</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">brueke</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bruki</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*brukiz</i>.

***brevet.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:brevet.html>brevet</a> (44015)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">brevete</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:brevet.html>brevet</a></i>. The sense “papal brief” <a href = vnd.unilang:comes.html>comes</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">brevetum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brevet.html>brevet</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brevet.html>brevetten</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">brevets</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A formal document, such as a certificate or licence.</li>
<li>A permit or licence allowing one to use certain vehicles or engage in certain activities, now especially in relation to aicraft, diving, swimming <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in Belgium</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> and sometimes mopeds.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bewijs.html>bewijs</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A papal <a href = vnd.unilang:brief.html>brief</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:brevet.html>brevet</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span> <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:diploma.html>diploma</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarbij.html>waarbij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bevoegdheid.html>bevoegdheid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitoefenen.html>uitoefenen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:functie.html>functie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verleend.html>verleend</a></li></ol>

***briefs.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:briefs.html>briefs</a> (132805)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:briefs.html>briefs</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">plural of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:brief.html>brief</a></i></span></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">usually  in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A short, close-fitting type of <a href = vnd.unilang:underpants.html>underpants</a>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Despite being a single item of clothing, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:briefs.html>briefs</a></i>—like <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pants.html>pants</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">trousers</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:underpants.html>underpants</a></i>, amp;c.—are considered to come in "<a href = vnd.unilang:pairs.html>pairs</a>" and are counted using the phrase "pair(s) of".
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i>See</i> Thesaurus:underwear</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:briefs.html>briefs</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Third-person singular simple present indicative form of <span class="mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:brief.html>brief</a></span></span></li></ol>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brief.html>brief</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">letter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bus.html>bus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">box</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***brig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:brig.html>brig</a> (70766)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Abbreviated from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">brigantine</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">brigantino</i>; in sense “jail”, from the use of such ships as prisons.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:brig.html>brig</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">brigs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A two-masted vessel, square-rigged on both foremast and mainmast</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A jail or guardhouse, especially in a naval military prison or jail on a ship, navy base, or (in fiction) spacecraft.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco"><a href = vnd.unilang:brig.html>brig</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">bryggja</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*brugjǭ</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bridge</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:brig.html>brig</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">brigs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Northern_Ireland" class="extiw" title="w:Northern Ireland">Northern Ireland</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Northern_England" class="extiw" title="w:Northern England">Northern England</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Bridge.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1790</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Burns" class="extiw" title="w:Robert Burns">Burns, Robert</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tam_o%27_Shanter_(poem)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Tam o |  Shanter (poem)"><a href = vnd.unilang:tam.html>Tam</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a>' Shanter</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Now do thy speedy utmost, <a href = vnd.unilang:meg.html>Meg</a>, / And win the key-stane of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:brig.html>brig</a></b>;</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Clipping of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:brigadier.html>brigadier</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:brig.html>brig</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">brigs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:brigadier.html>Brigadier</a>.</li></ol>
</body>

***bril.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bril.html>bril</a> (2397)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">beril</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:beryl.html>beryl</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">beryllus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:beryl.html>beryl</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">βήρυλλος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bḗrullos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Prakrit" class="extiw" title="w:Prakrit">Prakrit</a></span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">वैडूर्य</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vaidurya</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a cat's eye gem; a jewel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dravidian_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Dravidian languages">Dravidian</a></span>. Probably named after the city <i>Velur</i> (modern day <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Belur</i>) in southern India. The first glasses, manufactured in Italy around 1300, <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> made of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:beryl.html>beryl</a></i>. The meaning “toilet seat” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> younger and derived from the similarity in shape to a single eyeglass. The word forms a doublet with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">beril</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:beryl.html>beryl</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/brill_(fish)" class="extiw" title="w:brill (fish)"><a href = vnd.unilang:brill.html>brill</a> (fish)</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/brill_(fish)" class="extiw" title="w:brill (fish)">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p>Possibly from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cornish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Cornish language">Cornish</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="kw">brilli</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mackerel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="kw">brithelli</i>, plural of <i class="Latn mention" lang="kw">brithel</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mackerel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="kw">brith</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spotted</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:brill.html>brill</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">brills</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:brill.html>brill</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A type of flatfish, <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Scophthalmus_rhombus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Scophthalmus rhombus"><i>Scophthalmus rhombus</i></a></span>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Abbreviation of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">brilliant</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:brill.html>brill</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:brill.html>brill</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:brill.html>brill</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Wonderful, amusing. ***brimstone.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:brimstone.html>brimstone</a> (30034)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">brymston</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">brimston</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">bremston</i>, forms of <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">brinston</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">brenston</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">bernston</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">brynstān</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:brimstone.html>brimstone</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">burn-stone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:brian.html>brian</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">stone</i>, or <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">burn</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">stone</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">brunstane</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:brimstone.html>brimstone</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">brennisteinn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sulfur, <a href = vnd.unilang:brimstone.html>brimstone</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bernstein</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:amber.html>amber</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare also <span class="Latn" lang="en">brimfire</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">burn</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">stone</span>.
</p><p>Once a synonym for "sulfur", the word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> now restricted to Biblical usage.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:brimstone.html>brimstone</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">brimstones</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The sulfur of Hell; Hell, damnation.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1590</b>,  Edmund Spenser,  <cite>The Faerie Queene</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">For griefe thereof, and diuelish despight, / From his infernall fournace forth he threw / Huge flames, that dimmed all the heauens light, / Enrold in duskish smoke and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:brimstone.html>brimstone</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:blew.html>blew</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1667</b>,  John Milton,  <cite>Paradise <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>Lost</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Till, as a signal giv'n, th' uplifted Spear / Of their great <a href = vnd.unilang:sultan.html>Sultan</a> waving to direct / Thir course, in <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> ballance down they light / On the firm <b><a href = vnd.unilang:brimstone.html>brimstone</a></b>, and fill all the Plain; / A multitude.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1854</b>,  Charles Dickens,  <cite>Hard Times</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">[W]<a href = vnd.unilang:hen.html>hen</a> he [the Devil] <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> aweary of vice, and aweary of virtue, used up as to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:brimstone.html>brimstone</a></b>, and used up as to bliss [...]</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1916</b>,  James Joyce,  <cite>A Portrait of the Artist as a Young <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>Man</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">But the sulphurous <b><a href = vnd.unilang:brimstone.html>brimstone</a></b> which burns in hell <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a substance which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> specially designed to burn for ever and for ever with unspeakable fury.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Sulfur.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1816</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:walter.html>Walter</a> Scott,  <cite>The Antiquary</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:weel.html>Weel</a> I wot I wad be broken if I <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> to gie sic weight to the folk that come to buy our pepper and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:brimstone.html>brimstone</a></b>, and suchlike sweetmeats.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1838</b>,  Charles Dickens,  <cite>Nicholas Nickleby</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> think, young <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>, that <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> go to the expense of flower of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:brimstone.html>brimstone</a></b> and molasses, just to purify them.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A whore.
<ul><li><b>1763</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_Boswell" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:James Boswell">James Boswell</a>, in Gordon Turnbull (ed.), <i>London Journal 1762–1763</i>, Penguin 2014, p. 237:
<dl><dd>I <a href = vnd.unilang:went.html>went</a> to the park, picked up a low <b><a href = vnd.unilang:brimstone.html>Brimstone</a></b>, called myself a Barber, amp; agreed with her for <a href = vnd.unilang:sixpence.html>Sixpence</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:went.html>went</a> to the bottom of the park, arm in arm, amp; dipped my machine in the Canal […].</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Used attributively as an intensifier in exclamations.</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1852</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Charles_Dickens" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Charles Dickens">Charles Dickens</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bleak_House" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bleak House">Bleak House</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">You are a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:brimstone.html>brimstone</a></b> pig. You're a head of swine!</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1852</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Charles_Dickens" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Charles Dickens">Charles Dickens</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bleak_House" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bleak House">Bleak House</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">You're a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:brimstone.html>brimstone</a></b> idiot.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1913</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_C._Lincoln" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Joseph C. Lincoln">Joseph C. Lincoln</a>,  chapter 7, in  <cite><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL5535161W"><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. Pratt's Patients</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I made a speaking trumpet of my hands and commenced to whoop “Ahoy!” and “Hello!” at the top of my lungs. […] The Colonel woke up, and, after asking what in <b><a href = vnd.unilang:brimstone.html>brimstone</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the matter, opened his mouth and roared “Hi!” and “Hello!” like the bull of Bashan.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>The butterfly <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Gonepteryx_rhamni" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Gonepteryx rhamni"><i>Gonepteryx rhamni</i></a></span> of the Pieridae family.</li></ol>
